 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Fiscal 2021 Second Quarter Results Exceed Expectations </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Company Raises Guidance for Fiscal Year </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Second quarter results, year-over-year, including discontinued operations </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Total earnings per share (EPS), including discontinued operations, increased 10.9&nbsp;percent to $1.19, compared
to $1.07 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter; total adjusted EPS decreased 7.5&nbsp;percent to $1.40, down 8.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Second quarter results, year-over-year, from continuing operations </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

excluding sales from discontinued operations of $4.8&nbsp;billion </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

10.1&nbsp;percent to $1.26, down 10.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting an estimated adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of 40 to 45 cents per share </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Additional highlights </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$72&nbsp;million compared with the same period a year ago; Free cash flow was $1.9&nbsp;billion, up $85&nbsp;million year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

date, including 4&nbsp;million in March </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fiscal 2021 outlook </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-to-high</FONT></FONT> single digit growth in constant currency adjusted EPS from both total and continuing operations </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>CEO Transition </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">On March&nbsp;15, Rosalind Brewer succeeded Stefano Pessina as the company&#146;s chief executive officer and
joined the WBA board of directors; Pessina transitioned to the role of executive chairman of the board </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>$6.5&nbsp;billion divestiture
of Alliance Healthcare on schedule to close before the end of fiscal 2021 </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Financial presentation changes: assets being divested are moved to discontinued operations </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill., March&nbsp;31, 2021&#151;Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced financial results for the second quarter of fiscal
2021, which ended Feb. 28, 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Overall, we have achieved a good financial quarter with results well ahead of expectations, despite significant
impacts from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> and we have raised our full-year EPS guidance. I am optimistic about our ability to drive sustainable, long-term value for our shareholders, while acknowledging that there is still work
to be done to stabilize the base business,&#148; said Brewer. &#147;I will continue to review closely all our initiatives, strategies and opportunities to capitalize fully on the incredible potential in front of us. Our team will move swiftly and
decisively to best serve the needs of our patients, customers and communities around the world, at this critical time and beyond.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial Reporting Revisions for Pending Disposition of Alliance Healthcare Businesses </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On Jan. 6, 2021, WBA announced the sale of the majority of the company&#146;s Alliance Healthcare business and a portion of the Retail Pharmacy International
segment&#146;s businesses in Europe to AmerisourceBergen for $6.5&nbsp;billion. Upon closing, the company will account for the transaction as a business disposition. Until closing, the related assets, liabilities and operating results will be
reported as discontinued operations and are reflected as such in the company&#146;s second quarter financial results. As a result of the transaction, the company has reorganized its remaining businesses into two reportable operating segments, United
States and International. Corporate-related overhead costs are recorded separately and included in consolidated continuing operations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of
Second Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA had fiscal 2021 second quarter sales from continuing operations of $32.8&nbsp;billion, an increase of 4.6&nbsp;percent from
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, and an increase of 3.5&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>, reflecting strong International segment growth, aided by the
company&#146;s joint venture in Germany, and the United States segment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income from continuing operations was $832&nbsp;million in the second
quarter, compared with $1.1&nbsp;billion in the same quarter a year ago. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations was $1.2&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 22.5&nbsp;percent on a reported currency basis and a decrease of 22.9&nbsp;percent on
a constant currency basis. The decreases reflect adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impacts in the United States and International markets partly offset by cost savings related to the company&#146;s Transformational Cost
Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total net earnings attributable to WBA, including discontinued operations, increased 8.4&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter
a year ago to $1.0&nbsp;billion, reflecting a gain from the sale of a portion of the company&#146;s equity method investment in Option Care Health and a lower effective tax rate driven by discrete items, partly offset by lower operating income.
Total adjusted net earnings in constant currency decreased 10.2&nbsp;percent to $1.2&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total earnings per share<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2 </SUP>(EPS) in the second quarter increased 10.9&nbsp;percent to $1.19, compared to $1.07 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Total adjusted EPS decreased 7.5&nbsp;percent to
$1.40, down 8.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net earnings from continuing operations in the second quarter increased 6.3&nbsp;percent
compared with the same quarter a year ago to $922&nbsp;million. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations decreased 12.1&nbsp;percent to $1.1&nbsp;billion, down 12.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same quarter a
year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">EPS from continuing operations increased 8.7&nbsp;percent to $1.06. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $1.26 compared with $1.41 the
same quarter a year ago, a decrease of 10.1&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and a decrease of 10.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash
provided by operating activities was $1.4&nbsp;billion in the second quarter and free cash flow was $1.1&nbsp;billion, a $5&nbsp;million decrease compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of Fiscal 2021 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Year-to-Date</FONT></FONT> Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales from continuing operations in the first six months of fiscal 2021 were $64.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of 4.8&nbsp;percent from the same period a year
ago, and an increase of 4.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income from
continuing operations in the first six months of fiscal 2021 was $298&nbsp;million, a decrease of 85.5&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago mostly due to a charge in the first quarter from the company&#146;s equity earnings in
AmerisourceBergen. Adjusted operating income from continuing operations in the first six months of the fiscal year was $2.4&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 17.2&nbsp;percent from the same period a year ago on a reported basis, down 17.6&nbsp;percent on
a constant currency basis. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the first six months of fiscal 2021, total net earnings attributable to WBA, including discontinued
operations, decreased 59.9&nbsp;percent compared with the same period a year earlier, to $718&nbsp;million. Total adjusted net earnings in constant currency decreased 12.2&nbsp;percent to $2.3&nbsp;billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total EPS<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>, including discontinued operations, decreased 58.8&nbsp;percent to $0.83. Total adjusted EPS
decreased 9.3&nbsp;percent to $2.62, down 9.8&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In the same time period, net earnings from continuing operations
decreased 67.5&nbsp;percent compared with the same period a year earlier, to $531&nbsp;million. Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations decreased 13.7&nbsp;percent compared with the same period a year ago, to $2.0&nbsp;billion, down
14.3&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">EPS from continuing operations for the first six months of fiscal 2021 decreased 66.7&nbsp;percent to
$0.61, compared with the same period a year ago. Adjusted EPS from continuing operations was $2.36, a decrease of 11.4&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and a decrease of 12.0&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis reflecting adverse <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impacts of 70 to 75 cents per share. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $2.6&nbsp;billion in the
first six months of fiscal 2021, an increase of $72&nbsp;million from the same period last year, and free cash flow was $1.9&nbsp;billion, an increase of $85&nbsp;million from the same period a year ago. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Company Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company raised fiscal 2021 guidance
to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-to-high</FONT></FONT> single digit growth in constant currency adjusted EPS from both total and continuing operations. Previous guidance was for low single-digit growth. The
revised guidance reflects first-half performance above expectations and anticipated strong growth in the second half of the fiscal year. The situation continues to be fluid in the second half due to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Boots UK online sales doubled in the second quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Driving the Transformational Cost Management Program </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">The company is on track to deliver in excess of $2&nbsp;billion in annual cost savings by fiscal 2022.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Segments </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>United
States: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The United States segment had second quarter sales of $27.3&nbsp;billion, an increase of 0.4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including the adverse impact of store optimization programs and the 2020 leap day. Comparable sales increased 2.0&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter
reflecting a 4.5&nbsp;percent increase in comparable pharmacy sales and a 3.5&nbsp;percent decline in comparable retail sales. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Within comparable sales,
prescriptions filled in the second quarter decreased 1.1&nbsp;percent from a year earlier, including a combined negative impact of 480 basis points from an exceptionally weak cough, cold and flu season and reduced doctor visits. Total prescriptions
filled in the quarter decreased 2.8&nbsp;percent, compared with the same quarter a year earlier. The number of prescriptions filled was 288.5&nbsp;million, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT>
equivalents. Pharmacy sales, which accounted for 74.9&nbsp;percent of the segment&#146;s sales in the quarter, increased 3.0&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The segment&#146;s retail prescription market share on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> adjusted basis in the second quarter decreased
approximately 30 basis points over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to 20.9&nbsp;percent, as reported by IQVIA, including the impact of store optimization programs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales decreased 6.6&nbsp;percent in the second quarter compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, including adverse
impacts from the store optimization programs and the 2020 leap day. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable retail sales decreased 3.5&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a
year ago, reflecting the weaker cough, cold and flu season, which negatively impacted growth by 350 basis points. Comparable retail sales, excluding tobacco and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes,</FONT> decreased 2.7&nbsp;percent. Within
comparable retail sales, discretionary categories continued to decline, with beauty decreasing 8.8&nbsp;percent. Excluding the impact of seasonal flu, sales in the health and wellness category increased 9.1&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 2.2&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago and adjusted gross profit decreased 3.2&nbsp;percent, in both cases
primarily driven by pharmacy reimbursement pressure, retail volume and pharmacy volume, partly offset by pharmacy procurement, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccines and testing, and retail margin. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second quarter SG&amp;A increased by 3.3&nbsp;percent, and adjusted SG&amp;A increased by 2.1&nbsp;percent, reflecting
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related costs, including approximately $80&nbsp;million of costs relating to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">roll-out</FONT> of the vaccination program, as well as higher growth investments. These
increases were partly offset by cost savings related to the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the second quarter decreased
21.8&nbsp;percent to $828&nbsp;million from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating income decreased 18.2&nbsp;percent, to $1.2&nbsp;billion, reflecting <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT>
related impacts and pharmacy reimbursement pressure, partly offset by pharmacy procurement and cost savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>International: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The International segment had second quarter sales of $5.4&nbsp;billion, an increase of 32.6&nbsp;percent from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a favorable currency impact of 8.7&nbsp;percent. Sales increased 23.9&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, entirely due to the company&#146;s new joint venture in Germany,
which was consolidated as of November 2020. Excluding incremental sales from the joint venture, International segment sales on a constant currency basis declined 9.9&nbsp;percent, mainly due to a 17.8&nbsp;percent decrease in Boots UK sales
resulting from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related impacts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales increased 3.2&nbsp;percent compared
to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting favorable timing of National Health Service (NHS) reimbursement, and stronger pharmacy services, which mitigated the impact of lower prescription volume. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK comparable retail sales decreased 17.9&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> continued to impact footfall, particularly in major high streets, and in train stations and airports. The recovery in footfall trends seen in early autumn was set back by the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-introduction</FONT> of stricter restrictions beginning in November. However, Boots.com continued to perform very strongly with sales up 105&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, partially offsetting the reduced footfall. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK continued to gain market share in the
beauty category, but restrictions due to the pandemic impacted all other categories, reflecting the shift in buying habits to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-stop</FONT> grocery shopping. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 9.2&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago, including a favorable currency impact of 4.2&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross
profit decreased 13.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis reflecting lower UK retail sales and pharmacy volumes, partly offset by the favorable timing of NHS reimbursement and by incremental gross profit associated with the Germany joint
venture. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SG&amp;A in the quarter decreased 7.2&nbsp;percent from the prior year quarter to $973&nbsp;million, including an adverse currency impact of
4.2&nbsp;percent. On a constant currency basis, adjusted SG&amp;A decreased 9.6&nbsp;percent. Both decreases reflect short-term cost mitigation actions and cost savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program, partly offset by higher
SG&amp;A associated with the formation of the Germany joint venture. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income decreased 24.0&nbsp;percent to $106&nbsp;million, including a
favorable currency impact of 4.4&nbsp;percent. On a constant currency basis, adjusted operating income decreased 31.8&nbsp;percent, reflecting strict <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> restrictions in the UK, partly offset by decisive
cost management actions and strong Boots.com performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA will hold a conference call to discuss the second quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, March&nbsp;31, 2021. The conference call will
be simulcast through the WBA investor relations website at: <U>http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. A replay of the conference call will be archived on the website for 12 months after the call. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The replay also will be available from 11:30 a.m. Eastern time, March&nbsp;31 through April&nbsp;7, 2021, by calling +1 800 585 8367 within the U.S. and
Canada, or +1 416 621 4642 outside the U.S. and Canada, using replay code 1550649. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots Alliance
(Nasdaq: WBA) is a global leader in retail and wholesale pharmacy, touching millions of lives every day through dispensing and distributing medicines, its convenient retail locations, digital platforms and health and beauty products. The company has
more than 100 years of trusted health care heritage and innovation in community pharmacy and pharmaceutical wholesaling. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Including equity method
investments, WBA has a presence in more than 25 countries, employs more than 450,000 people and has more than 21,000 stores. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA&#146;s purpose is to
help people across the world lead healthier and happier lives. The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA is a Participant of the United Nations
Global Compact and adheres to its principles-based approach to responsible business. WBA is included in FORTUNE&#146;s 2021 list of the World&#146;s Most Admired Companies.* This is the 28th consecutive year that WBA or its predecessor company,
Walgreen Co., has been named to the list </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More company information is available at <U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com.</U> </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures
calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not
calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. Please refer to the notes to the &#147;Net Earnings and Diluted Net
Earnings (Loss) Per Share&#148; reconciliation table on page 14 for definitions of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures and related adjustments presented in this press release. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s
financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide
additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press
release. The company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis (including the information under &#147;Company Outlook&#148; above) where it is unable to provide a
meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet
occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is
unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially
from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company also presents certain information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such
constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding
the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the company&#146;s United States and International segments, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least 12
consecutive months without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past 12 months as well as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for
the first 12 months after the relocation. Acquired stores are not included as comparable sales for the first 12 months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable
retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions, respectively. Comparable retail sales for previous periods have been restated to include <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. The method of calculating
comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to the International segment, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and comparable retail
sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant currency calculations.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company considers
certain metrics, including all comparable metrics, number of prescriptions, number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the
company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the
company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP
financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other companies. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The Company recognized equity losses in AmerisourceBergen of
$1,373&nbsp;million during the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2020. These equity losses are primarily due to AmerisourceBergen recognition of $5.6&nbsp;billion, net of tax, charges related to its ongoing opioid litigation in its financial
statements for the three months period ended September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program and Store Optimization Program charges are costs associated with a
formal restructuring plan. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets and inventory
valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangibles assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks and contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from
the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the company&#146;s GAAP financial statements, the revenue generated by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the
related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset becomes impaired or the estimated useful life of
an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to measure acquired inventory at fair value. The fair value of the
inventory reflects cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments excludes the expected profit margin component from cost of sales recorded under the business
combination accounting principles. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Certain legal and regulatory accruals and settlements relate to significant charges associated with certain
legal proceedings. The Company excludes these charges when evaluating operating performance because it does not incur such charges on a predictable basis and exclusion of such charges enables more consistent evaluation of the Company&#146;s
operating performance. These charges are recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The company&#146;s United States segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if the United States segment inventory is accounted for using <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and manufacturer pricing practices, which may be
impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger, acquisition and
divestitures related activities. These costs include all charges incurred on certain mergers, acquisition and divestitures related activities, for example, including costs related to integration efforts for successful merger, acquisition and
divestitures activities. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing and complexity of the underlying merger, acquisition and divestitures related
activities and do not reflect the company&#146;s current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the company&#146;s net investments in
foreign subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within other income (expense). We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying
derivative instruments reflects the company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gain on sale of equity method investment. During the three months ended February&nbsp;28,
2021, the Company recorded a gain of $191&nbsp;million in Other income due to a partial sale of its equity method investment in Option Care Health. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">9</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax provision include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax provision commensurate with <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. tax law changes and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within income tax provision
(benefit). </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">10</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to post tax equity earnings from other equity method investments consist of the proportionate share
of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are
recorded within post tax earnings (loss) from other equity method investments. Although the company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating
to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations
in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other
contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;#&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;# </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">20 </P>

</DIV></Center>

</BODY></HTML>
</TEXT>
